THE STATE v. DOMNICA ALBU
Conducted by Registered Post under Provisional Order No.9
Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov — Registry of Record

────────────────────────────────────────────────
CHAPTER 13 — "A Form Filled In Wrong"
DELIVERY CYCLE No. 13    ·    Early December, the first ice skinning the slack water under the Podul Vechi, the Casimca too low and too cold to flood and somehow worse for it, the stove fed with the magistrate's wood and the office smelling of birch and damp wool
────────────────────────────────────────────────

BUNDLE — CYCLE 13. Released this cycle, in the order below:
  1. Magistrate's Notice — Defense Witnesses Invited to Declare — T. Lupu → The Proceeding — [REGISTERED No. 0520]
  2. Form 12-B "Declaration of Posting" — V. Andrei (mother) → registry — filled irregularly; accepted — [REGISTERED No. 0521]
  3. Routing Slip 0523 — G. Enescu, Postmaster (on the acceptance of the irregular declaration)
  4. Deputy's Internal Note — M. Brânză → file / union — objecting to the acceptance — [no registration number; internal]
  5. Routing Slip 0524 — G. Enescu, Postmaster (on the deputy's objection, and on the matter of the margins)

HELD (carried to Cycle 14):
  · Domnica Albu's account of the testing of the water (the "self-testing" letter) — held one cycle — slip 0524 — to release Cycle 14, the Podul Vechi being under water at the eastern crossing and the carrier turned back

NOT ENTERED ON THE PROCEEDING (no registration number; office discretion):
  · The reverse leaf of Form 12-B No.0521, on which V. Andrei continued writing past the printed form and into the place where there is no form — retained, by the stove, for reasons set out in slip 0524

────────────────────────────────────────────────


[REGISTERED No. 0520]   [POSTMARK: VÂLCOV CENTRAL, the 2nd of December — received 09:20, during the four hours, by foot, the wire being down at the seat since the frost]

[The following is written on the back of a printed bill of sale, the front of which reads, faintly through the paper: AURORA STALL — PIAȚA LIPSEI — birch, dry, one ster — PAID. Lupu's hand, cramped, the loops not quite closing.]

MAGISTRATE'S NOTICE
To the Proceeding, and to the defence, by way of the registry —

The defence having opened, and the accused being entitled under Order No.9 to call such persons as may speak to the matter, the court invites any person with knowledge of the night of the 14th of September to declare it by Form 12-B, in the manner of the prosecution's witnesses, and to post the same to the registry, who will certify the fact of posting.

I add, as I am obliged to add and as the form does not, that the court is aware the defence has no advocate and no clerk and no means of summoning anyone, and that a notice of this kind, in a town of this size, is mostly a way of asking the willing to find their own courage. The court has no power to compel a witness and less power to protect one. It can only promise to read what comes.

By the authority vested — and I will not, this cycle, append the usual remark about by whom, the joke having worn as thin as the gloves —

T. LUPU, Magistrate
Vâlcov

[margin, in Lupu's hand, smaller:] Registry — I am out of forms again. If a witness comes to you without one, give her one of yours and charge it to the court. The court will pay you in the spring, when it pays me.


[REGISTERED No. 0521]   [POSTMARK: VÂLCOV CENTRAL, the 4th of December — received 09:05]

[The form is a standard Form 12-B, "Declaration of Posting," printed in the ministry's grey ink, its fields ruled in boxes. It has been filled out in pencil, hard, the lead breaking through in places. The printed text is in ROMAN; the filled-in matter is rendered as written.]

MINISTRY OF JUSTICE — PROVISIONAL ORDER No.9
FORM 12-B — DECLARATION OF POSTING
(to be completed by the declarant and countersigned by the postmaster as to the fact of posting only)

NAME OF DECLARANT: ┃ Veronica Andrei ┃

OCCUPATION: ┃ alive, thanks to the accused, and a washerwoman ┃

ADDRESS: ┃ the low houses past the tannery, you know the ones ┃

MATTER DECLARED (state briefly): ┃ I have nothing brief. See the back. The box is the wrong size for it. ┃

I DECLARE THAT THE FOREGOING WAS POSTED BY ME ON THE DATE BELOW, AND THAT THE CONTENTS ARE TRUE TO THE BEST OF MY KNOWLEDGE.

[the printed oath has been struck through, once, with the pencil, and beside it written:]

I will not declare it true to the best of my knowledge. I do not have knowledge, I have a son. I will declare it true the way you declare a fever true, by living through it. If the court wants the other kind of truth it can ask the plant, who keeps a log.

DATE: ┃ the night my Petrică could not stop being sick, plus three months ┃

SIGNATURE: ┃

[The box marked SIGNATURE contains, in place of a name, a full sentence, written small to fit and still overflowing the rule:]

On the night the water went wrong my boy Petrică drank from the Aleea Salciilor well the way he has drunk from it his whole short life and by the dark he was bringing up everything in him and then bringing up nothing, which is worse, and I carried him to the school because the school is the only door in this town that has ever opened to me, and the teacher came out in her nightdress and her coat over it and she looked at him once and she said to me, Veronica, this is the water, do not give him the water, not the well and not the plant's, give him nothing from the ground until I send word — and then she went out into the dark herself, toward the plant, and I do not know what she did out there and I am not going to pretend to the court that I do, but I know my son was dying at the supper hour and at the morning he was weak and alive, and I know that nobody from the plant came, and nobody from the pharmacy came, and the number you call for the doctor answers only between six and ten and my son did not arrange to be sick between six and ten. So if the court is asking me whether the teacher poured something in the water, I will tell the court I was not at the water, I was at my son. And if the court is asking me whether the teacher is the kind of person who poisons a town, the court has not met her, and I have, and I am signing this with the whole thing instead of my name because my name is not the evidence. She is.

[at the foot of the form, below all the boxes, in the postmaster's violet:]

Countersigned this 4th day of December as to the fact of posting only. — G. ENESCU


ROUTING SLIP 0523.
Released this cycle, with the magistrate's notice: Form 12-B No.0521, the declaration of V. Andrei.
Reason of record:

The form came to my window this morning in a state I am required to describe and would rather not, the description being the kind a clerk reaches for to keep a feeling at arm's length, and the feeling having got past the arm. She had filled it in wrong. She had filled in every box wrong. Where the form asks the declarant's occupation and means *what does the state pay you to be,* she has written what she is, which is a person the accused kept alive, and *a washerwoman* added afterward as though her trade were the afterthought and her survival the main fact, which — the form being indifferent and I being not — it is.

The question before this office is narrow and I will keep it narrow, the way a man keeps to the path because he is afraid of the field. The question is not whether her declaration is true. Order No.9 does not ask me that and has wisely never asked any postmaster that, we not being equipped, our equipment being a date-stamp and a stove. The question is whether *Form 12-B No.0521 is a valid declaration of posting* such that I may register it and certify it and let it onto the proceeding.

I have read §6 of the Order, which governs the form, eleven times, looking for the clause that says a declaration is void if the declarant declines the printed oath, or void if the signature box does not contain a name, or void if the matter spills past the boxes the ministry drew for it — and §6 says only that the declarant shall complete the form and the postmaster shall certify *that it was posted.* It does not say the form must be completed *correctly.* It does not define correctly. The men who drew the boxes assumed that anyone who could write would write inside the lines, the way they assumed a town would have a courthouse and a sequence would never be in question. The ministry has ruled the boxes and forgotten that a box is only a suggestion to a person with enough at stake.

So: she struck the oath. I note this. The printed oath asks her to declare the contents true *to the best of her knowledge,* and she has refused the words and supplied her own — *true the way you declare a fever true, by living through it* — which is not, I think, a lesser oath. It is a more dangerous one. The state's oath protects the witness; it says *only to the best of my knowledge,* which is the witness leaving herself a door. She has nailed her own door shut. A woman who swears she has no knowledge, only a son, has told the court she cannot be impeached on the facts because she has declined to claim any, and has put in their place a thing the court has no instrument to weigh and no clause to dismiss. I have certified the posting of cleverer documents written by people with advocates and worse ones written by people with degrees.

As to the signature. The box is empty of a name and full of a sentence. I rule — and I am aware that a postmaster ruling anything is its own small absurdity, the ruling being mine and the appeal being to no one — that the sentence in the signature box is a signature, on the ground that a signature is a mark a person makes that no one else could have made, and there is no one else in the Republic who could have made this one. Câmpeanu signs his name and a hundred prosecutors could sign it the same. Olaru signs his name and his clerk could forge it and has, very likely, more than once. This woman has signed with the only thing that is unmistakably hers, which is the thing that happened to her, and I find that more securely her hand than any flourish. *As it is unmistakably hers* — let that be the reason of record and let the deputy make of it what the deputy will.

Filed in good order. — G.E.


[The following is not registered to the proceeding. It is an internal note. It was left on the registration desk, weighted under the date-stamp, where the postmaster would find it. It is typed — the deputy owns the only working machine in the building, a thing he mentions — on a half-sheet headed with the union's device.]

INTERNAL NOTE — to the Registrar, copy to file, copy to the District Union (Branch of Posts & Custody)
From: M. Brânză, Deputy Sorter
Re: Acceptance and registration of Form 12-B No.0521

Registrar —

I object, for the record, to the registration of the above as a valid Declaration of Posting, and I am copying this to the union and to the file so that the objection is on paper before the document is, and cannot later be said to have been an afterthought of mine.

The grounds are not complicated and I have set them in order:

1. The declarant did not complete the prescribed oath. She struck it through. A Form 12-B with the oath struck is, on the plain face of §6, not a Form 12-B; it is a letter on a form.

2. The signature field does not contain a signature. It contains prose. I am aware the Registrar has ruled the prose to be a signature "as it is unmistakably hers." I would respectfully observe that *unmistakably hers* is a standard the Registrar applies, that no clause supports, and that the Registrar — uniquely in this district — is in a position to apply to whichever documents he chooses, the documents passing through his hands and no one else's.

3. I note, copying again to file, that this is the second instance in the defence phase in which the Registrar has resolved a procedural doubt in the accused's favour by reading the Order generously. The first was the holding of the records-request to the plant until it could be released ahead of the accused's account. I do not allege. I log. I have been told the union expects a clean chain of custody in time of emergency, and a clean chain is one where the rules close the same door for everyone, regardless of whose son.

Logged. Copied to the union. For the record.
M. Brânză


ROUTING SLIP 0524.
On the deputy's note of this date; and on the matter of the second leaf of No.0521; and on the hold of the accused's testing-letter.
Reason of record:

The deputy is right. I want that in the file before anything else I say, because he is going to be in the file regardless and I would rather meet him there honestly than be caught out by him later, the way a man would rather walk into the cold water than be pushed. He is right that *unmistakably hers* is a standard I invented and that no clause supports it. He is right that I am the only man in the district who can apply such a standard, the documents passing through my hands and no one else's, as he says, and as he is careful to say twice. He is even right — and this is the part that costs me — that this is the second time I have read the Order generously toward her, and that a clean chain is one where the same door shuts for everyone.

He is right about all of it, and he has understood none of it.

Here is the thing the deputy cannot see, because he logs and does not read. He thinks the danger is that I bent a rule for her. The danger is smaller and worse: the rule did not need bending. §6 truly does not require the form to be filled in correctly. I have not stretched the Order; I have only declined to stretch it the deputy's way, which would be to read into §6 a requirement the ministry never put there — *that a declaration be void unless the declarant submits to the box.* He wants me to invent a rule that voids her. I have refused to invent a rule. He calls my refusal a favour. That is the whole disease of this proceeding in a single misunderstanding: by now, even *not* tipping the scale looks like tipping the scale, because the scale has been in my hands so long that my open palm and my thumb have begun to weigh the same.

I do not know how to get out from under that, and I am recording that I do not know.

On the second leaf. Veronica Andrei did not stop at the foot of the form. She turned it over, and on the reverse — where there is no field, no rule, no box, no place the ministry made for anything — she kept writing, smaller and smaller, the pencil going soft and then gone, the last lines pressed in without lead at all so that they can only be read by holding the leaf to the window and reading the trough the pencil dug. I have held it to the window. I am not going to transcribe it onto the proceeding. It is not a declaration; it adds nothing the state can use and it would only give the deputy a second document to log. But I will set down, because the form has a line for *particulars* and because no one but me reads this line, the one part I could read in the trough without lead:

*she argues the way the teacher writes her letters, the washerwoman, untrained, the same way, building a thing out of what happened to her and refusing to call it less than evidence, and I have read both their hands this winter and I will say here where no one is listening that the schoolteacher and the washerwoman are the only two people in this whole file who write as though a sentence were a kind of debt you owe the person reading it. Everyone else writes to be done with me. These two write to be read by me. I keep the second leaf by the stove with the rest of what I cannot deliver and should not have. It will be warm. Order No.9 says nothing about warm.*

On the hold. The accused's account of the testing of the water — the letter in which, I am given to understand, she describes what she did at the intake and how she came to do it — was posted from Aleea Salciilor and reached the eastern crossing of the Podul Vechi on the 3rd, where the carrier found the old bridge under water at its low end, the river being too low to flood and the ice having dammed it at the pylons instead, which is a new way for the Casimca to ruin a delivery and I note it for the record as a thing the bridging-committee did not foresee, the committee not having foreseen the bridge. The carrier turned back with the letter dry under his coat but a day late. I hold it one cycle, to Cycle 14. I record, because the deputy would otherwise record it for me, that the hold is not of my choosing this time — the river chose it — and I record also, more quietly, that I notice I am relieved, and that I do not entirely trust my relief, a held letter being a letter I still control and a delivered one being a letter gone out of my hands into hers.

That is the part the deputy will never log, because there is no box for it, on his form or on mine.

Filed in good order. — G.E.

[margin, G.E., at the foot, in violet, very small:] Twelve times now, the one by the stove — not 0431, the new one, the washerwoman's reverse leaf. I am not going to call it the same thing. I am only going to note that I have begun to keep a count of a second one, and that a man who keeps two counts is no longer counting envelopes. He is counting the people in his town who still believe a letter goes to someone.

THE STATE v. DOMNICA ALBU
Conducted by Registered Post under Provisional Order No.9
Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov — Registry of Record

────────────────────────────────────────────────
CHAPTER 14 — "Water Damage"
DELIVERY CYCLE No. 14    ·    Early December, the Casimca over its low bank again, the Podul Vechi awash to the second plank, the first thin ice forming overnight in the gutters of Strada Făgădău and gone by ten
────────────────────────────────────────────────

BUNDLE — CYCLE 14. Released this cycle, in the order below:
  1. Routing Slip 0541 — G. Enescu, Postmaster — opening the cycle; condition of the sack ex Podul Vechi
  2. Defense Letter No.5 (Domnica Albu → the registry) — "on the testing of the water by my own hand" — [REGISTERED No. 0536] — RECEIVED WATER-DAMAGED; delivered as received
  3. Postmaster's Certified Transcription of No.0536 (the legible parts, with losses marked) — office exhibit, [No. 0536-t]
  4. Magistrate's Query No.0538 (Lupu → Domnica) — on the re-service of damaged matter
  5. Routing Slip 0543 — G. Enescu — closing the cycle

HELD (carried to Cycle 15):
  · The child's note (Ilinca Pop) — received Cycle 9, held since — reason of record: "pending the order in which it can be read" — slip 0492, carried again
  · Domnica records-request, No.0489 — released Cycle 12; the plant's filtration records still not produced by Aurora — re-demand pending

NOT ENTERED ON THE PROCEEDING (no registration number; office discretion):
  · One sheet, the postmaster's hand, reconstructing the lost lines of No.0536 — destroyed at the stove the same night it was written — not retained — recorded here only as having existed

────────────────────────────────────────────────


ROUTING SLIP 0541.
Released, this cycle: nothing yet. Opened to record the condition of the sack.

Reason of record:

The Podul Vechi went under to the second plank in the night between the cycles, the Casimca having risen four fingers on the gauge stone at the foot of Strada Cazaclia — the same gauge the engineer's report read, four springs ago, the morning it gave up on the courthouse. Everything east of the river comes over that bridge or it does not come. The carrier, Frunză, brought the eastern sack across at first light with the water at his knees, which I record not to praise him, the man being paid in bread and not enough of it, but because the sack came over *wet,* and a wet sack is a fact the registry must enter before it enters anything the sack contained.

I have logged, in thirty years, every kind of ruin a letter can arrive in. Frost. Mice. The damp of a coat. Once a whole month's eastern post black at the edges from a barn it had sheltered in that burned around it — every letter legible, every letter smelling of the fire, and a man cannot read that his daughter is married off a page that smells of a burned barn without the barn getting into the marriage. I delivered them anyway. The decree does not provide for smell.

It does not provide for water either. Order No.9 §11 says the registry shall deliver every instrument *as registered,* and is silent — it is always silent at exactly the place a man needs it to speak — on what the registry does when the river has registered something of its own on top of the state's. There is no clause for the river. The men who wrote the order had a courthouse and a bridge that held.

In the sack, among the ration lists and a seed catalogue addressed to no such address, one registered letter for the proceeding, in the hand I now know better than I know my own — the schoolteacher's, No.0536, her account, the magistrate having asked her by query last cycle to set down *whether and how she tested the water before she touched it,* this being the whole question of the thing, intent living or dying in the answer. She posted it in the last of November; the river turned the eastern sack back at the bridge twice before it would let it cross, so that a thing written in one month arrives in the next, the postmark washed to *...ovem...* and the man who reads it left to certify, against the calendar, that late-posted is not late-written. She wrote it. The river read it first.

I have not opened it past what the damage opened for me. I am opening it on the next slip, in the record, so that what I did to it and what the water did to it are kept on separate lines and no man reading this later can say the postmaster and the river were the same author.

The state today is not the order. The river is the order. I am recording that I know the difference, on the one day it is true.

Filed in good order. — G.E.


[REGISTERED No. 0536]   [POSTMARK: VÂLCOV EAST — the date washed; legible only "...ovem..." — POSTED late November, the river then turning the eastern sack back twice at the Podul Vechi; RECEIVED here Cycle 14, early December, the posting-to-delivery gap entered per Slip 0541]   [WATER-DAMAGED — endorsement at foot]

[The letter is reproduced as received. Where the water took the words, the loss is marked. The registry has added nothing and removed nothing. — G.E.]

To the registry, and to You who decide when I am heard —

I have been asked, in a fair question and the first fair question the court has put to me, whether I tested the water before I did the thing the State says I did. I will answer it the way I would answer a child who asked me how I knew the stove was hot: I will tell you how I knew, and you will see that knowing is not the same as [illegible], and that a person can be certain of a danger and still be [water-lost] of the cure.

On the evening of the fourteenth the well on Aleea Salciilor [water damage — two lines lost] . . . and Miron, who is nine and was my pupil before he was my evidence, had been sick since the noon. His sister Ilinca came for me because there was no one [illegible] would come. I went with what a schoolteacher has, which is a kettle, a clean spoon, and the habit of reading instructions, and I [water-lost].

First I tasted it. I know You will say a person of education should not taste a thing she suspects, and You would be right, and I did it anyway, because a teacher learns nothing she has not first [illegible] put in her own mouth. It was bitter. Then it was the taste of coins, which I have written to You before and which You will remember if You are the reader I think You are. Then — and this is the part I beg you to keep, because it is the part the State will not ask for — it was the taste of *nothing,* and I . . . [water damage — three lines lost] . . . becomes a question, and I will not let a child drink a question.

So I tested it the second way, which is the only way a person without a laboratory can. I [water-lost] from the Izvorul Aurora end of the run, where the plant draws, and a measure from our well, and I . . . [illegible] . . . the silver spoon, which my mother left me and which is the only assay a poor woman owns, and the spoon came out of the plant's water [water damage — the line lost entirely] . . . and out of ours [illegible]. You do not need to be a chemist to read a spoon. You need to be a person who has been poor long enough to have only the spoon.

I am told the prosecutor has written, in a paper I am not permitted to see whole because the registry has blacked the heart of it — and I do not complain of the blacking; whoever holds the pen that blacks it has, I think, blacked it [illegible] to keep me from sounding like a recipe, and if that is so, then thank you — that I "introduced a compound." I did. I will not stand on the word *introduced* as though a verb could save me. I poured a measure of the white into the run above the intake, having read the instruction on the tin three times and a fourth, and having [water damage — two lines lost] . . . the dose for a cistern, not a river, and a river is not a cistern, and I knew it, and I did it anyway, because the four hours were not yet open and the health office answers only the four hours and Miron could not wait for six in the morning to be sick correctly.

Did it help. You will want me to say it helped. I cannot say it helped. I can say I have lain awake on the question the way I imagine You lie awake on Yours — for I have decided You have one, no man reads letters the way You read mine who is not lying awake on something — and the honest end of my lying awake is this: I do not know whether I cleaned the water or [water-lost] it worse for an hour to clean it for a week. The chemistry does not love me enough to tell me. Neither, I notice, does the court.

What I know is what I was *for.* I was for the boy. The State is trying a verb, *poisoned,* and I am offering it a preposition, *for,* and these do not fit in the same box on any form the Republic prints, and that is not my failure of grammar. It is theirs.

[water damage — the close, perhaps four lines, lost entirely]

. . . and so I remain, with a strange and improper warmth toward a room I have never seen and a man I am not supposed to believe is reading this —

[signature washed; a stain in the shape of the name; the descender of the *b* survives]
 . . . [Albu]
Aleea Salciilor, behind the school

P.S. — The Podul Vechi has flooded every autumn since the Tsars, and the Republic, I am told, has resolved the matter by appointing a committee. I send my account over a bridge a committee owns. If half of it drowns, mark it not against me but against the committee, and tell them a schoolteacher says they have had four hundred years and one river and have lost to the river.

[FOOT ENDORSEMENT, registry hand:] Received water-damaged ex Podul Vechi. Damage pre-existing to office handling. No matter added or removed. Reproduced as received. — G.E.


[Office exhibit. No registration to the proceeding; filed alongside No.0536 as the registry's certified reading. — G.E.]

POSTMASTER'S CERTIFIED TRANSCRIPTION OF No.0536
Made under Order No.9 §11, "delivery as registered," the original being partly illegible by water.

I certify the following, and only the following, as to the document No.0536:

1. That it arrived water-damaged, the damage being the river's and not the office's, per Slip 0541 and the foot endorsement.

2. That I have transcribed every word the water left and have written *[illegible]* or *[water-lost]* where it took them, and that I have written nothing in the gaps. This is the difficult part to set down and I will set it down plainly: I can read this hand. I have read this hand more than I have read any hand alive. There were places where the sense of a lost line stood up out of the words on either side of it so clearly that I could have supplied it, the way a man who has known a song all his life can sing through a verse the gramophone skips — and I did not supply it. To supply it would have been to forge. The registry does not forge. It is the one thing I have never done and the one thing I will not do even here, even for her, even when the forgery would only have been the truth.

3. That I am therefore obliged to deliver to the magistrate a document in which the words *did it help* survive and the answer the writer gave to them does not — the river having taken her answer and left her question — so that the most exonerating account in the file reaches the court as a doubt instead of a defense. I want it on the record that this was done by water and not by the registry. For once in this proceeding the order of the truth was decided by something that cannot be tried. I find I resent the river for it the way a man resents a rival who is honest. It did in one crossing what I have spent fourteen cycles learning to do with a stove and a rack, and it did it without a reason of record, and it does not have to lie awake.

4. That the postscript, concerning the bridge and the committee, survives entire and legible, the river having spared the only joke and drowned the only defense, which is either the river's idea of mercy or its idea of wit, and the registry is not qualified to say which.

So transcribed and certified, the original retained on the proceeding, the damage entered. — G.E.


[REGISTERED No. 0538]   [POSTMARK: PIAȚA LIPSEI sub-office — by hand, no machine date]

[On the reverse of a firewood receipt. The receipt reads, in another hand: STALL 6, PIAȚA LIPSEI — "1 ster beech, 1 ster birch wet — sold to the parish, winter early — PAID." The query is written over the wood. — registry note]

MAGISTRATE'S QUERY No.0538
In the matter of The State v. Domnica Albu
From the office of the Magistrate, T. Lupu, sitting at Piața Lipsei this being the only roof with a stove I am permitted

To the accused, by way of the registry —

Madam,

The registry has delivered to me your account of the testing of the water, No.0536, and has delivered with it its own certificate that the account arrived damaged by the river at the Podul Vechi, with passages lost. I have read what survives twice, my hands permitting, which lately they do not always.

I am obliged to put to you a hard thing, and I will put it without the courtesy formulas, the office being cold and the formulas being expensive and, as you have more than once observed, vested in no one. The thing is this: the law cannot weigh what it cannot read. The passage in which you answer your own question — *did it help* — is among the passages the water took. As the document stands, the court has your question and not your answer, and a question, in law, is the absence of a defense and not the presence of one.

You are therefore entitled, under Order No.9, to a re-service: to write the account again, whole, and post it fresh, and the registry will deliver the new copy in place of the drowned one. I would counsel it. I would counsel it strongly, were counsel a thing an unpaid magistrate is permitted to give the accused; call it instead the observation of an old man who sells wood and has watched the river take a courthouse one plank a year and would not like to watch it take a defense.

But I will not order it, and I will tell you why, because you have corrected my spelling four times in this proceeding and earned, I think, a straight reason. To re-serve is to cross the Podul Vechi again, which floods, and to wait a cycle, perhaps two, and the State across the river is pressing this office to *conclude* — the prosecutor's word, underlined twice in the last wire as though underlining were evidence. Every cycle you spend re-serving is a cycle the State spends arguing that delay is itself a confession. I have seen the order of a thing decide the thing more than once. I do not say it has happened here. I say I am tired enough to notice that it could.

So I leave it to you: the drowned account, delivered now, ambiguous; or the whole account, delivered late, into a court being told that lateness is guilt. I am sorry to be the man who hands you that choice. The river handed it to me. I am only the next in the line.

Reply within two delivery cycles, the Podul Vechi permitting, which lately it does not.

By the authority vested — vested, I confess again, by no one currently paying me, and conducted today between the sale of one ster of wet birch to the parish and the next —

T. LUPU
Magistrate, sitting at Piața Lipsei
[in the margin, a fainter hand:] Forgive the wood under the words. The office had no forms and I had no gloves. The parish wanted the receipt back. They did not get it. Justice has kept it. It is the warmest thing in the room.


ROUTING SLIP 0543.
Released, this cycle: No.0536 (water-damaged, as received), its transcription 0536-t, and the magistrate's query 0538. All delivered together. Held: nothing new. The child's note carried again.

Reason of record:

I am required to record my reasons and I have one and it is short and I do not like it.

I delivered the drowned letter.

I could have held it. There is a colourable ground, and Mihail has already written it up at his window before the ink on my endorsement was dry — *Item No.0536 received in damaged condition; registry recommends nondelivery pending re-service; postmaster overruled own recommendation without recorded necessity; copied to the union, for the record* — Mihail being a man who logs the way other men breathe, and who would have me hold the letter so that the proper procedure could be observed and the accused could spend two more cycles in the cold being correct. He is not wrong that holding it is the cleaner course. He is wrong, as he is always exactly wrong, about what cleanliness is for.

Here is the thing I am turning over, and I will turn it over on the form because the form is the only place in this building where a man is permitted to turn anything over. For fourteen cycles I have been the order. I told myself, on a slip much like this one, that recording a fraud is not committing one, and I have begun to suspect the slip was the fraud and the man was the record. Tonight the river took the pen out of my hand. Something with no reasons of record decided which half of her would reach the court, and it chose the half that does not save her, and it did not consult me, and I find — this is the part I am ashamed to set down and am setting down — I find I am *jealous.* Not of a man. Of a river. It arranged her without loving her and without lying about it, and I have never once managed both.

So when the choice came — deliver the drowned account now, ambiguous, or hold for the whole one and let the State call the wait a confession — I did the thing that for once does not require me to be the order. I delivered what arrived, in the condition it arrived, on the day it arrived. I took my hands off. The river had already taken them off; I only agreed.

It does not help her. I want that on the record beside the fact that I did it. The honest act and the unhelpful act are the same act this cycle, which is new, and which I do not have a clause for, and which I think is what honesty is going to feel like from here, now that I have noticed I am capable of the other thing.

As to the matter I will not enter on the proceeding and have already destroyed:

I sat last night with the drowned letter and the lamp and I did the thing the transcription says I did not do — I supplied the lost lines. Not on the document; never on the document. On a separate sheet, in my own hand, for no one, the way a man hums the verse the gramophone skips. I read the words on either side of the loss after *did it help* and I wrote what she would have written, because I know the hand and I know the woman the hand is making and I could hear the answer standing in the gap as clearly as I have ever heard anything: that she did not know, that she would never claim to know, that she had decided a long time ago that she would rather be uncertain and have acted than be certain and have watched, and that this was the whole of her and she was not going to pretend it added up to innocence because adding up was the court's hunger and not hers.

I wrote four lines like that. They were warmer than anything the river left. They were, I think, *true* — truer than the transcription, which is only accurate. And then I held them to the stove, because a reconstruction in the postmaster's hand of the accused's lost defense is precisely the kind of true thing that, entered, would be a forgery, and, kept, is just my company. I burned it. I am recording that it existed and that I burned it. It is the nearest I have come to writing her a letter, and I did the only thing I have ever done with the letters I most want to send, which is not send them — which I learned a long time before this proceeding, in another winter, over another thing I did not deliver and will not write here.

I have read No.0536 — what the river left of it — more times tonight than I am going to count, the count having stopped meaning what it meant. She wrote *You,* with the capital, four times before the water took the rest, and each time it was not the court she meant and not the registry she meant. I am not going to tell her she is right. I am going to deliver her question without her answer, and let the magistrate make of it what a cold tired man makes of a cold drowned thing, and tomorrow when the eastern sack goes back over the Podul Vechi I will watch the water come up the gauge stone at the foot of Strada Cazaclia toward the courthouse it already has a third of, and I will think — God help the registry — that the river and I want the same woman and only one of us has the decency to be a river about it.

Reply from the accused expected within two cycles. The Podul Vechi permitting. It will not permit. Nothing here permits. We proceed anyway; it is the only verb the office owns.

Filed in good order. — G.E.

THE STATE v. DOMNICA ALBU
Conducted by Registered Post under Provisional Order No.9
Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov — Registry of Record

────────────────────────────────────────────────
CHAPTER 15 — "The Child at the Fence"
DELIVERY CYCLE No. 15    ·    Early December, the Casimca skinned with grey ice at the margins, snow not yet down but promised, the school on Aleea Salciilor shut three days for want of coal, the stopped clock on the Palatul de Justiție wearing a cap of frost at 11:40
────────────────────────────────────────────────

BUNDLE — CYCLE 15. Released this cycle, in the order below:
  1. Magistrate's Query No.0552 — T. Lupu → The Proceeding (concerning the completeness of the defense's witnesses; written, again, on the back of a firewood receipt) — [REGISTERED No. 0552]
  2. Deputy Sorter's Internal Note (4th) — M. Brânză → the file, copied to the District Postal Union — [internal; logged, not registered to the proceeding]
  3. Routing Slip 0556 — G. Enescu, Postmaster
  4. Routing Slip 0557 — G. Enescu, Postmaster (supplemental, opened the same night)

HELD (not released; carried forward, cycle undetermined):
  · One note in a child's hand, addressee "Teacher," received unregistered the 2nd of December, folded small and carried in by hand — the matter set out in slip 0556 — held pending the order in which it can be true. Not yet entered on the proceeding.

NOT ENTERED ON THE PROCEEDING (no registration number; office discretion):
  · The graded spelling examination on the reverse of the said note (94 marks, in the accused's hand) — physically inseparable from the note, and therefore held with it — slip 0556

────────────────────────────────────────────────


[REGISTERED No. 0552]   [POSTMARK: VÂLCOV CENTRAL, the 1st of December — received 09:40, during the four hours, carried by foot from Piața Lipsei]

[The query is written on the reverse of a printed receipt. The printed side reads, in part: PIAȚA LIPSEI — STALL No.6 — RECEIVED of the bearer, for FIREWOOD (birch, seasoned, one ster) — PAID. The magistrate's hand begins beneath the word PAID and runs up into the margins where the form leaves him room.]

MAGISTRATE'S QUERY
In the matter of The State v. Domnica Albu

To the Registry, and through the Registry to any party able to answer —

The office will forgive the stationery. The court is out of forms again, and out of much else; I write on what the stall provides, the stall providing more reliably than the Ministry, which I record without bitterness, a man past sixty having no more use for it than for the gloves he also lacks.

I have now before me the defense as it has reached me: the accused's own account of the night; the mother's declaration, which the registry has ruled valid notwithstanding that it overflows every box the form provides and signs itself with a sentence; and the letter the river took at the Podul Vechi, of which I have the postmaster's faithful transcription and the gaps the water left, which gaps I am instructed by no clause to interpret and have therefore interpreted, against my office, in the only direction a man can interpret a wound, which is to ask who made it.

My query is narrow, and I put it to the registry because the registry is the only party that sees every letter before I do:

Is the defense's roster of witnesses complete? I ask not idly. The State has produced the pharmacist, the neighbour, the manager, and the manager's log. The defense has produced the accused, the mother, and a drowned page. It is not my place to seek out witnesses for either side; it is my place to ask whether any have been *received and not yet placed before me.* If the answer is none, I will close the defense and proceed. If the answer is otherwise, I would know it before I write what I am, God help me, nearly ready to write.

I append no time-limit. The accused has taught half this town its letters, and I find I do not wish to hurry the reading of what those letters were for.

By the authority vested — vested, I confess, by no one currently paying me —

T. LUPU, Magistrate
Piața Lipsei, the firewood being wet this week and sold cheap


[INTERNAL — Deputy Sorter's Note, 4th. Logged in the office day-book. Copied, per the deputy's standing practice, to the District Postal Union, Grievance Channel.]

NOTE FOR THE FILE — M. Brânză, Deputy Sorter
Re: an unregistered item received the 2nd December and not entered

I record the following so that it is recorded by someone other than the postmaster, the postmaster's records being, in my respectful and repeated submission, a private literature and not a public one.

On the 2nd of December, at the deputy's window, a child of the Aleea Salciilor school — Pop, the younger, the girl — delivered by hand a folded paper addressed to "Teacher." I received it. I logged it in the day-book at 16:10, item unregistered, sender a minor, addressee the accused. By the plain words of Order No.9, any matter touching the proceeding is the proceeding's, and a paper from a witness who was at the fence that night — for the child says she was at the fence; she said so at my window, in front of two people queuing for stamps — touches the proceeding as surely as the pharmacist's letter does.

I gave the item to the postmaster, as procedure requires, for registration.

It has not been registered. It is the 5th of December. Three cycles have turned. I have asked twice. I am told it is "held pending the order in which it can be true," which is a sentence, and I am a postal officer and not a critic, and a sentence is not a registration number.

I therefore log, formally, that the Vâlcov registry is in possession of a witness statement from a child who placed herself at the scene, and has not entered it, and that the postmaster's reason for not entering it is that he has not yet decided what it ought to mean. I make no accusation of forgery, theft, or destruction; I have none to make; in eleven years beside him I have never known him alter a single mark, and I say so for the record because the record should be fair even where it is damning. He does not falsify. He *withholds.* I am no longer certain the difference is one the Union, or the District, or a child's mother, will find comforting.

Copied to the Union. For the record. — M.B.


ROUTING SLIP 0556.
Held. Not registered to the proceeding. Carried forward, cycle undetermined.
Reason of record:

The deputy is correct in every particular and wrong in the only one that matters, which is the assumption that a thing's being true is the same as its being ready.

I will set down what the item is, the form asking for the Particulars, and the form being the one place in this building where I am permitted to tell the truth at the length the truth requires.

It is a single leaf, folded to the size of a child's palm and folded again, the creases soft from being carried somewhere warm — against the body, I think; it came to me with no chill on it at all, which the deputy will not have noticed, the deputy reading paper for its contents and not its temperature. On the front, in pencil, pressed so hard in places the lead has silvered and in places torn the fibre: *to Teacher.* Capital T. She has made the T the way the accused makes the C in "the Court" — a capital out of fear, and a capital out of love, and a child cannot yet tell which of the two she is afraid of, so she gives the word both and lets the reader sort it.

On the reverse is a spelling examination. I did not look for it; it was simply the other side of the only paper the child had. The accused graded it. Ninety-four marks, and beneath the mark, in the accused's own hand, the violet of the school not the violet of the state but close enough that for a moment my chest did a thing I will not describe in an official document: *lovely work, Ilinca.* So I am holding, the registry is holding, the State of which I am the registry is holding, a possible conviction for the poisoning of a town paper-clipped — not paper-clipped, the child has no clips, fused, two faces of one sheet — to a gold star.

Now the note itself. I transcribe it exactly, the misspellings being the most honest spelling in the file, because she has not yet learned which words the State prefers and so has used her own:

  *deer Teacher i seen you that nite at the fenss. i seen you pore the wite stuf in the water out of the jug. and i seen you grab Miron by his cote and pull him bak hard so he wuld not go in the water. wich did you do first i cant member wich was first. mama says dont rite to you but i am riting becas you are my Teacher and i am not afrade of the water no more becas you fixt it or you did the other thing i dont no wich. dont be in truble. 94 was my best ever. Ilinca*

I have read it four times, which for once is not a confession but an arithmetic of dread, and here is the dread:

She saw both. She saw the white poured into the water — which the State needs, which is purchase made flesh, the compound from Costea's pharmacy entering the intake by the accused's own hand, the very act, witnessed, undeniable, in a child's pencil that no advocate will impeach because no one impeaches a nine-year-old who graded ninety-four. And she saw the same hand seize a drowning boy by the coat and haul him back from the bank — which the defense needs, which is the whole of the defense, the saving hand, the woman who went to the dark not to kill a town but because a child was already at the water and she was the only one who came. Both. In one leaf. In one sentence each, side by side, and the child cannot remember which was first, *i cant member wich was first,* and neither, the registry observes, can the registry.

This is the thing I have understood tonight, and I record it because the form has a line for the matter and the matter is my own ruin: it is not the facts that decide this. The facts are settled. She poured. She pulled him back. Both happened; the child saw both; no one disputes a word. What is not settled — what cannot be settled by any amount of inquiry, by the inspector the district keeps threatening to send, by the Judge's stamp if it ever comes down off its ration of violet — is *which one is the story and which one is the detail.* And that is not a question of fact. That is a question of order.

If this leaf is read after the pouring has been established — after Costea, after the sighting, after her own account of the white in the jug — then "i seen you pore the wite stuf" is the verdict and "pull him bak" is a mitigating flourish, the kind of thing the guilty do on the way to doing the thing they came for, and the child has handed the State its eyewitness and a gold star to make it unbearable. If this leaf is read after the saving has been established — after the mother, after the drowned page, after a town that taught its children at her knee — then "pull him bak hard so he wuld not go in the water" is the truth of her and "pore the wite stuf" is what saving the water looked like to a frightened child who did not know that the white was meant to clean it. Same leaf. Same ink. Same ninety-four on the back. The girl wrote the truth, the whole truth, and the truth, being whole, points both ways, and I am the only person in the Republic who decides which way it is allowed to point, because I am the one who decides when it arrives.

So I am not registering it. Not tonight, not this cycle, possibly not for many. I am not destroying it — the deputy will note, the Union will note, the inspector when she comes will note, that I have not destroyed it, that it sits folded and warm in the Hold where the deputy logged it arriving, every mark intact, the ninety-four intact, *lovely work, Ilinca* intact. I am holding it for the order in which it can be true. There is no such order yet. The defense is half-built. To place this leaf now, into a file the State has spent eleven cycles teaching the town to read as guilt, is to hang her with a child's hand. I will not do it now. I will do it — I am writing the sentence and I am watching myself write it — when I have built the house in which "she pulled him back" is the room you stand in, and "she poured the white" is only the window you see the water through.

I am aware of what that sentence is. The magistrate has asked me, this very cycle, on the back of a firewood receipt, whether any witness has been *received and not yet placed before him.* The honest answer, the four-word answer the office is famous for, is: *one has. A child.* And I am going to answer him otherwise, or rather I am going to answer him not at all and let the silence stand as none, and the silence will be the first true lie of my life, because I have never written a false word and tonight I will withhold a true one, and a withheld truth, the deputy is right, the deputy is unbearably right, is going to feel to the child's mother exactly like the other kind.

A note on the warmth, which the form permits because the form permits everything and forbids only the kraft envelope. The leaf came in warm because she carried it against herself, this child, walking up Strada Făgădău in December to the deputy's window to write to a Teacher she has been forbidden to write to, because she is not afraid of the water any more, *becas you fixt it or you did the other thing i dont no wich,* and she has solved in nine years and a 94 the entire case the State cannot solve with a prosecutor and a magistrate and an inspector and a stopped clock — *fixt it or the other thing, i dont no wich* — and she is not troubled by not knowing, she is only troubled that I might be in trouble, *dont be in truble,* and she does not know, she cannot know, that I am the trouble, that the trouble is the order, that the trouble is me.

I have read it now five times. The fifth was not arithmetic.

I note, finally, because the deputy has copied his note to the Union and a man should answer in the same book even if he never sends it: I have not registered envelope 0431 either, in fourteen cycles, and no one has logged me for that, because no one knows it exists, because it is not from a witness, it is from her, written before there was a case, addressed to "whoever this turns out to be," and that one I hold not for the order in which it can be true but because there is no order, in this world or the next, in which I am permitted to be the man it turns out to be. The child's leaf I hold to protect her. That one I hold to protect myself. I am no longer sure the second is the lesser crime.

Filed in good order. — G.E.


ROUTING SLIP 0557.
Supplemental. Opened the same night, an hour later, the stove gone to embers.
Reason of record:

I went back to register it.

I record this so that the record contains not only what I did but the thing I nearly did, the law being interested only in the former and a man, at one in the morning in a cold office, being interested in both.

I took the leaf out of the Hold. I uncapped the violet. I had the registration book open to the next clean line, 0558, and the pen down to the page, and I was going to give it a number — because the deputy is right, because the magistrate asked, because a child should not be the one paper in the file I treat as mine, because somewhere in this is the difference between the order I keep and the order I author, and I have stopped being able to find it. I had written the *0* of 0558. It is there now, a single violet zero with nothing after it, which I will leave, the way I left the back-dated gap on the indictment's aviz, because I do not erase the evidence of my own hesitations.

And then I read the back of it again. *Lovely work, Ilinca.* In her hand. And I understood that if I register it tonight — clean, numbered, in the order it arrived — it will be read this cycle, the town eleven cycles deep in guilt, and the child will have hanged her Teacher with a paper that also says she is not afraid of the water any more. The honest act and the merciful act have come apart in my hands, and I find I am not, after all, an honest man. I am a man who would rather be merciful and call it order.

So I capped the pen. I put the leaf back, folded, warm no longer, the office being cold and the body that warmed it a quarter-mile off on Aleea Salciilor under a roof that has no coal either. The zero stands in the book. The number does not follow it. The matter is held — pending the order in which it can be true — which is to say, pending me.

The deputy will report this. Let him. I have given him nothing to report but the truth, which is the only thing I have ever given anyone, and which I am learning, too late, can be administered like a poison: not by what you put in the water, but by when.

I have decided I am the order. I wrote that in October as a boast. I am going to have to find out, before this is over, what it costs to be the thing you decided to be — and whether a child who is not afraid of the water any more will forgive the man who held her sentence by the stove until it was warm and never let it arrive.

Filed in good order. — G.E.


[Margin, in violet, at the foot of slip 0556, added later, the hand smaller:]
She spells "remember" without the first r. *Member.* As in: a part of a body. As in: what the State will do to this case — take it apart at the joints and keep only the limb it can use. The child has misspelled her way into the truest word in the file and graded herself, by my count, a great deal higher than ninety-four.

CHAPTER 16 — "A Letter Grigore Can Tell Is Forged"
DELIVERY CYCLE No. 16    ·    Mid-December, the Casimca closed bank to bank now except the black seam down the middle where the current will not let it, the snow down at last and grey by noon, the Aurora No.4 stack smoking on a Sunday when by its own posted log it does not run on Sundays
────────────────────────────────────────────────

BUNDLE — CYCLE 16. Released this cycle, in the order below:
  1. Telegram TG-02 — District Seat → Vâlcov Central Sorting — [logged; not registered to the proceeding]
  2. Witness Letter "in the matter of the night of the 14th of September" — signed *N. Spânu, watchman* → The Proceeding — [REGISTERED No. 0561]
  3. Routing Slip 0563 — G. Enescu, Postmaster
  4. Registration Log — Central Sorting, Vâlcov (leaf for Cycle 16)

HELD (not released; carried forward):
  · The child's note, addressee "Teacher," unregistered, the void 0558 standing in the book — held, as before, pending the order in which it can be true — slip 0556/0557 refer

NOT ENTERED ON THE PROCEEDING (no registration number; office discretion):
  · The kraft envelope in which No.0561 arrived — retained, separately, as the only honest thing in the item — slip 0563

────────────────────────────────────────────────


[TG-02]   [LOGGED 08:50, within the four hours — District Seat to Vâlcov Central Sorting — transmission charges to the directorate]

TELEGRAM — DISTRICT SEAT TO VÂLCOV CENTRAL SORTING

REGISTRY VÂLCOV STOP MATTER ALBU DRAGS STOP FOURTH MONTH NOW STOP DISTRICT NOTES DEFENSE PRODUCING SYMPATHY NOT FACTS STOP REMIND REGISTRY EVIDENCE IS RECEIVED NOT CURATED STOP A WITNESS COMES FORWARD THIS WEEK FROM PLANT QUARTER STOP REGISTER AND DELIVER WITHOUT DELAY STOP ORDER NO 9 ALLOWS NO REGISTRY TO WEIGH TRUTH ONLY TO CERTIFY POSTING STOP CONCLUDE BEFORE THAW STOP RESOURCES LIMI[ink failed here]ED STOP

[At the foot, in violet, G.E.:] The district announces my witness to me before my witness has reached me, which is a thing the post is not supposed to permit and which the telegraph, being faster and stupider, permits all the time. They knew on the 14th of December that a watchman would come forward. The watchman's letter is postmarked the 15th. I am told what is coming before it comes, by people who insist the order of things carries no meaning, and I am to register and deliver it *without delay*, which is the one instruction in this telegram I will obey, the others being beneath the dignity of a man who has read Order No.9 more times than the Ministry has.


[REGISTERED No. 0561]   [POSTMARK: VÂLCOV EAST, the 15th of December — received 14:20]
[Item arrived in a KRAFT envelope. The envelope is forbidden under Order No.9 §5 ("envelopes of the kraft sort are forbidden as unbecoming the dignity of the state"). The envelope is retained per slip 0563. The letter itself is on white stock and is registered, the office having no clause by which to refuse a letter for the sins of its envelope.]

To the Proceeding, care of the Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov, and to the Magistrate appointed thereto —

I, the undersigned, employed as night watchman at the Uzina de Îmbuteliere "Aurora Nr.4," make this declaration of my own free will and of my own personal knowledge, having no interest in the matter save the public good and a clear conscience.

On the night of the 14th of September I was at my post upon the access road, Drumul Aurora, the hour being shortly after eleven. I saw the accused, DOMNICA ALBU, schoolteacher, approach the intake works of the said plant. I saw her clearly, the moon being sufficient. She carried a vessel. She bent at the intake. She poured from the vessel into the water with both hands and with deliberation, looking about her as a person looks who does not wish to be observed. I called out. She fled toward the willows on Aleea Salciilor. I am certain of her identity, having known her by sight these many years, and I am certain of the act, having seen it with my own two eyes and being a sober man.

I make this declaration late, with regret, having feared for my position; but a man cannot sleep with such a thing unsaid, and the public health being the highest law, I set it down now that justice may be done and the guilty party held to account for the poisoning of the town's water and the suffering thereby occasioned.

Respectfully submitted in the interest of public order and the safety of the community,

NICOLAE SPÂNU
Night Watchman, Aurora Nr.4
Drumul Aurora


ROUTING SLIP 0563.
Released this cycle — registered, delivered, on the proceeding — over my own certain knowledge that it is false.
Reason of record:

Let me first say the only thing the State will care that I say, which is the thing I have done: I have registered the letter signed *N. Spânu* as No.0561, and I am delivering it this cycle to the magistrate and to the accused, in good order, without delay, exactly as the district instructs and exactly as Order No.9 requires, there being no clause in that instrument, none, I have looked again tonight, by which a registry may refuse a letter on the ground that the registry does not believe it. I am to certify that a thing was posted. It was posted. I certify it. That is the whole of my office and I have discharged the whole of it.

Now let me say the thing the form has a line for and the State has no interest in, which is that the letter is a forgery, and that I know it the way I know my own name, and that I am going to write down how I know it, because if I am to deliver a lie under my own hand and seal I will at least leave, beside it, in violet, the record that the hand which delivered it was not deceived. A man may be made an instrument. He need not be made a fool. The distinction is the last property I own.

I have sorted the mail of this town for thirty years. There is no hand in Vâlcov I have not held a hundred times. I know the doctor's prescriptions and the widow Frumușel's complaints to the council and the way the boy at the dairy crosses his sevens. I know them the way a shepherd knows sheep that to you are all one colour. And I am telling the record that there is no *N. Spânu* whose hand this is, and here is how the page tells me so, line by line, because I read this letter the way she taught me to read — carefully, and then again, and then a third time, the third time not for what it says but for what it *is.*

The ink first. It is a blue-black, machine-made, of the kind that comes from the capital in glass bottles and which no man on Drumul Aurora has ever owned, the men out there writing, when they write at all, in pencil or in the cheap brown ink the co-operative sells from a barrel. A night watchman at Aurora does not keep capital ink. A man who keeps capital ink does not work nights at Aurora. The ink and the post-mark are quarrelling, and I believe the ink.

The hand next. It is too good. That is the tell, and it is the one the district will never understand, because the district believes a clean hand is an honest one. This hand is *educated* — it keeps its line, it spaces its words like a clerk, the loops of its *l* and its *d* are closed and even, the down-strokes weighted the same on the first word and the last, which is a thing a tired hand never does and an unpractised hand cannot do. A real watchman writing a real accusation at the end of his own courage writes worse at the bottom than at the top, the hand failing as the nerve fails. This hand does not fail. It is the same at "Respectfully submitted" as at "I, the undersigned." It was not written by a frightened man unburdening a conscience. It was written by a steady man performing one, slowly, with good light and capital ink, and the steadiness is the fingerprint.

The pressure third. I read the back of it with my thumb, the way I have read ten thousand backs of pages, and the pressure is uniform — pressed even, letter to letter, the mark of a man copying, not composing. A man saying a true and terrible thing presses hard where the horror is — on *poured*, on *fled*, on the woman's name — and light where the throat-clearing is. This page is pressed flat as a deed. He was not feeling the sentences. He was tracing them.

The paper fourth, and here the forger has been careful: good white stock of the lawful grammage, correct in every particular Order No.9 specifies — a man took the trouble to learn which weight of paper justice is permitted to be done on, and obey it. And then he put it in a kraft envelope.

I want this in the record because it is, in its way, the funniest thing that has happened to me since October, and a man should be allowed to laugh once in a slip even on a night he is being made a liar. The forger studied the dignity of the state down to the grammage of the leaf. He matched the white. He matched the weight. He invented a watchman and a moon and a vessel. And then he sealed all that labour inside the one envelope the law names, by name, as forbidden — the kraft sort, unbecoming the dignity of the state — the very envelope a man at the plant would have to hand because that is what the plant ships its bottles in, the cheap brown stock of the loading dock, and he reached for what was nearest and undid himself with it. He forged everything but the envelope, and the envelope is the only honest object in the item, because the envelope, at least, came from where the letter came from.

So I will tell you who I think made it, the form asking for *Particulars* and the particulars being mine to record though not to act upon. I think it came from the plant — the leavings not of a frightened man on Drumul Aurora but of an office: capital ink, an even clerkly line, the kraft from the loading dock, the watchman announced by district telegram a day before he writes, and a nine-thousand-and-rising reason to nail this case to a schoolteacher before anyone asks why the stack at Aurora smokes on a Sunday the log says it does not run. I will not write the manager's name in the file, because I cannot prove it and because to write it would be to do, in the registry, the very thing being done to her — to deliver a name in the absence of a proof and let the order make it true. I have done that once, in October, on purpose, and I have not forgiven myself, and I will not buy my conscience back by aiming the same weapon at the man I happen to be right about. Being right is not a permission. It is only a heavier kind of restraint.

Here, then, is what I am, and am not, going to do.

I am not going to bury it. I do not bury things. The deputy will tell the Union, and the Union will tell the inspector who is coming, and they will find No.0561 registered and delivered in good order on the very cycle the district demanded it, and they will find nothing in the chain of custody amiss, and that is correct, because nothing in the chain of custody is amiss. The chain is clean. The letter inside it is rotten. That is the whole horror of my office, learned tonight in full: that I am the guardian of the *vessel* and have no warrant over the *water,* that I can certify perfectly the posting of a perfect lie. I once told this book that I would never need to forge a hand because I had learned them all. Tonight that learning is good for one thing only. It cannot save her. It can only let me suffer accurately — to know, to the loop and the down-stroke, exactly which lie I am carrying to her door under the seal of the state.

And I am not going to forge against it, either, which is the thing a cleverer and worse man would do — manufacture a second watchman, a contrary moon, an honest hand to cancel the dishonest one. I have the skill. I have, God help me, the ink. I will not. The one wall left standing in me is that I deliver what is, and arrange what is, and never once invent. Take that wall down and there is nothing between this office and the plant but a difference of motive, and motive is not a wall, motive is weather. She did not write to a forger. She wrote to a reader. I will stay the reader or I will stop being anything she would have addressed.

So I keep my one power, the only one, the small one, the whole of me: order. I cannot refuse the lie. I can choose what it arrives *beside.* I am releasing No.0561 this cycle — promptly, as ordered, so that no one can say the registry slowed a prosecution witness — but I am releasing it into a cycle I have salted. The magistrate already holds Domnica's own account of the night, in which she says she poured and says what the pouring was for; he holds the records-request the plant has never answered; he holds, in his own honest skull, the fact that I delivered him last week, that the Aurora log shows the intake "inspected daily" on three days the plant stood shut for St. Paraschiva. A man reading a watchman's accusation the same week he is chewing on a plant that inspects water it is not drawing — that man reads the watchman differently than a man reading him cold. I cannot strike the lie from the file. I can make sure it walks into a room where the questions are already standing up.

It is not enough. I am recording that it is not enough. A forgery delivered beside its own doubt is still a forgery delivered, and a town that has been four months learning to read her as a question will read one more accusation as one more weight on the side it already leans. I am doing the only thing my office permits and it is not enough, and the distance between *the only thing I can do* and *enough* is the exact size of the wound I have been carrying since October, and it does not get smaller, and I have stopped expecting it to.

One last particular, for the form, which asks and asks and never tires. The kraft envelope I am holding out of the file — not destroying; retaining; the office keeps what it does not enter — and I have set it on the cold end of the rack, away from the stove, because it does not deserve the warmth and because I do not want it near her letters. It is the truest thing in the item. It will be, when the inspector comes, the only object in this whole proceeding that says plainly where a paper came from. I will keep it the way you keep the one witness who cannot lie, the one who has no tongue and therefore cannot be made to perjure: a brown envelope from a loading dock, forbidden by §5, retained by me, the most honest document in *The State v. Domnica Albu,* and entered into nothing.

Filed in good order. — G.E.


[Leaf inserted by the office, in the postmaster's hand:]

[margin, G.E.:] The column is headed FROM. I have written *"N. Spânu, watchman"* in quotation marks, the quotation marks being the only honesty Order No.9 leaves me — I may not refuse the entry, but I am nowhere forbidden to set a name in the marks a man uses for a thing reported rather than a thing known. The register will show forever that the office logged this witness *as he gave himself,* not as he was. It is the smallest possible truth and it is the only one I had the room to file. A pair of inverted commas. Thirty years of knowing every hand in Vâlcov, and what it buys her, in the end, is two little marks around a name, set down by a man who could prove they belonged there and is not allowed to.


[INTERNAL — Deputy Sorter's Note, 5th. Logged in the office day-book. Copied, per the deputy's standing practice, to the District Postal Union, Grievance Channel.]

NOTE FOR THE FILE — M. Brânză, Deputy Sorter
Re: Registered item No.0561 (witness Spânu), Cycle 16

I record, for once, a regularity, the record having been so long a chronicle of the postmaster's irregularities that I wish it noted when he is, by the book, correct.

Item No.0561 was received the 15th December, registered the same day, and released this cycle without a hold. The district telegram TG-02 directed prompt registration and delivery; the postmaster complied; the chain of custody is, in this instance, unbroken and timely. I have no objection to log and I log that I have none.

I record, however, one thing I do not understand and therefore set down rather than interpret. The postmaster has retained the item's envelope — separately, unentered, on the cold rack — and has written across the day-book that it is "the most honest document in the proceeding." An envelope is not a document. It bears no statement. I have asked him what an envelope can be honest about. He answered that it can be honest about where it came from, which is, he said, "more than the letter inside it managed." I do not know what he means. I record that I do not. I record also that he registered the witness "in quotation marks," which is not a recognised registration practice and which I would ordinarily report as an irregularity, except that I cannot, in conscience, frame a man for the crime of punctuation.

Copied to the Union. For the record. He delivered the letter on time and to the book. I find, to my own surprise, that this troubles me more than his holds ever did. — M.B.
