POSTAL-UNION CIRCULAR No.7
From the Deputy Registrar, Vâlcov Central Sorting, in his capacity as union correspondent
To all district registries, and to file

RE: RESTORING CONFIDENCE IN THE REGISTRY

Following the conclusion of the proceeding *State v. Albu* and the departure of the Internal Order inspectorate, the deputy registrar wishes it recorded, for the benefit of the union and of any office that may in future operate under Provisional Order No.9, that the Vâlcov registry has been assessed IRREGULAR BUT REHABILITATED, that no dissolution will issue, and that the chain of custody is, going forward, to be maintained under refreshed procedure.

The deputy notes for the record that he raised, in good faith and at some cost to himself, the matter of irregular hold patterns; that he was, in substance, correct; and that the matter has nonetheless been closed without finding against any officer. He accepts this. He observes only that a registry is not a feeling. It is a rack, a stove, a book, and a man, and of these the man is the part most prone to warm in the wrong places. The union recommends, going forward, that reasons of record be confined to operational necessity.

He adds, in his own hand and not the union's, that he has worked beside the registrar eleven years and never once caught him in a forged figure or a missing letter, and that this is, he has come to understand, precisely the difficulty: a man you cannot catch is a man you cannot govern, and the registrar was never dishonest, only ungovernable, which the union has no form for. Copied to file. Copied to the union. For the record. — M.B.


[Reg. 0612]   [the summary leaf, prepared for the District Seat per TG-04, to be filed during the four hours, the terminal permitting]

SUMMARY LEAF FOR ARCHIVE
THE STATE v. DOMNICA ALBU — Disposition
Prepared by the Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov, at the instruction of the District Seat

The proceeding is closed. The magistrate's ruling, No.0610, bound the matter over neither convicted nor acquitted, and was dispatched for delivery to the accused. Delivery was not effected, the addressee having quit the address leaving no forwarding. Under Order No.9 §14 the ruling is, in consequence, of no force. The aviz de primire returned unsigned, no cause on the printed list applying. The Internal Order Directorate certified the proceeding procedurally concluded and was silent as to its legal conclusion. The seal VĂZUT / SEEN has not descended, the violet allocation being suspended this quarter.

The matter is therefore archived in the following state, which the office sets down plainly because the District Seat has asked for a summary and a summary should not flatter: a woman was charged with poisoning a town; the State assembled true facts against her and could not, with all its instruments, decide whether they amounted to a crime or to a rescue; it built a proceeding to answer the question; the proceeding answered nothing; and the answer, such as it is, is that the question has been disposed of without being settled, the disposal and the settling being, the office has learned this winter, two entirely different rooms.

The office forwards this leaf as instructed and retains the file.
For the registry — G. ENESCU, Postmaster.


[The following is the Dead-Letter Endorsement. It is the formula stamped on the undeliverable. The office uses it perhaps forty times a year, for the dead, the moved, the never-were. It is being used twice this cycle. The endorsements are entered first, the routing slip after, because the form is filled before the reason is given, always, and I will give the reason after, as I have given every reason for four months, into a field no one reads. — G.E.]


DEAD-LETTER ENDORSEMENT
Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov — Dead-Letter Drawer

ITEM: Statement of [the engineer], ex-Aurora Nr.4, re: the filtration intake — registered to the proceeding, held since autumn, cold end of the rack.
CAUSE OF NON-DELIVERY (registry to state):

   ☐  ADDRESSEE MOVED        ☐  ADDRESSEE DECEASED
   ☐  REFUSED                ☐  NO SUCH PROCEEDING

   [no box ticked]

[across the foot, in violet, small:]
   None of these, again, and this time the failure of the boxes is not the
   river's doing and not hers but mine. The proceeding exists; it is merely
   closed. The addressee — the proceeding itself, the file, the magistrate —
   is not moved, not deceased, not refusing; it is finished, and a finished
   proceeding cannot receive a document, the way a made bed cannot receive a
   guest. I consign this statement undeliverable not because there is no one to
   give it to but because I will not be the one to give it. The cause of
   non-delivery, stated truly, is the registrar. I am the cause. I tick no box
   because the form has no box for the man who runs it. To the Drawer. — G.E.

[STAMP: DEAD-LETTER — UNDELIVERABLE — CENTRAL SORTING, VÂLCOV — the 12th of February]


DEAD-LETTER ENDORSEMENT
Central Sorting Office, Vâlcov — Dead-Letter Drawer

ITEM: One letter, D. Albu, never registered to the proceeding — Envelope 0431 — at the Hold, by the stove, since the autumn — read [the count is no longer kept].
CAUSE OF NON-DELIVERY (registry to state):

   ☐  ADDRESSEE MOVED        ☐  ADDRESSEE DECEASED
   ☐  REFUSED                ☐  NO SUCH PERSON

   [no box ticked]

[across the foot, in violet, small:]
   This item was never on the proceeding and so was never, properly,
   undeliverable — a thing not entered cannot fail to arrive. I am endorsing it
   anyway, out of order, against procedure, because I want it in the same drawer
   as the rest of what I could not send, and the Drawer admits nothing without a
   cause, and the only honest cause is the one I have spent four years and four
   months refusing to write on a form: that the addressee of this letter is me,
   that it arrived, that it was delivered, that I received it eleven times and
   then past counting, and that I am consigning it undeliverable not because it
   did not reach its reader but because its reader cannot bear to let it leave
   the only room where it was ever true. NO SUCH PERSON is the nearest box and
   it is a lie; she was the truest person in the book. I tick nothing. To the
   Drawer, where it has, in the way that matters, always been. — G.E.

[STAMP: DEAD-LETTER — UNDELIVERABLE — CENTRAL SORTING, VÂLCOV — the 12th of February]


[Leaf inserted by the office, in the postmaster's hand:]

REGISTRATION LOG — CENTRAL SORTING, VÂLCOV
Registry of Record, The State v. Domnica Albu — FINAL LEAF
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 No.    | DATE      | FROM            | MATTER                       | STATUS
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 0610   | 24 Jan.   | Mag. Lupu       | The Ruling (Hotărârea)       | NOT EFFECTED — no force, §14
 0610-a | 5 Feb.    | carrier         | Aviz for 0610                | RETURNED unsigned
 0612   | 12 Feb.   | this office     | Summary leaf for archive     | Forwarded; file retained
 [eng]  | (autumn)  | ex-Aurora eng.  | Statement re: filtration     | DEAD-LETTER — undeliverable
 0431   | (autumn)  | D. Albu         | (never on the proceeding)    | DEAD-LETTER — undeliverable
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
The book is closed on The State v. Domnica Albu. Forty years this office has logged the births, the deaths, the deeds, and the seed catalogues of Vâlcov, and once a trial, and the trial is the only entry in the whole book that ends with no verb in the STATUS column that means a thing was decided. Delivered, returned, forwarded, undeliverable. Not one of them is *judged*. I leave the column honest. The river will have the building before the State has the answer, and the building is going faster. — G.E.


ROUTING SLIP 0660.
Status: CLOSING. Nothing held; nothing released to the accused, there being none. The rack, as to this proceeding, is empty for the first time since October. Reason of record — the last I will write into this file, and the longest the form has carried, the form having borne everything else and able to bear this.

I said last cycle I would do the thing I had been circling all winter and had not had the nerve to name, and that the form would have a line for it. The form has the line. It is the cause-of-non-delivery line on the Dead-Letter Endorsement, and I have filled it twice this morning, and I am about to tell the form why, which is the only confession this building was ever built to take.

In the autumn I held a witness against her so that her account would land first, and called it mercy, and it was. In the winter I held a child's note until the clause that saved her could be read as the governing one, and called it order, and it was a fraud, and it was also, I still believe, the truest reading of a true note. I held the engineer's statement — the one document in this whole file that points the slow hand of the poisoning back at the plant, at the intake, at the sludge let into the water for a buyer in the capital, at the man who has never once had to write his soul into a slip because he wrote it into a maintenance log and ruled it documented secure — I held that statement when releasing it would have given Lupu his struck paragraphs back and a name to aim the doubt at and might, might, have tilted the ruling toward *the plant did this, not the teacher.* I held the lever. And the verdict came, and went out, and bound her over to nothing, and reached a cold stove and a made bed and came back unsigned, and the lever is still in my hand.

So here is the choice the whole winter has narrowed to, and I want it on the record exactly, because Drăgan is gone and the district has disposed of the matter and Mihail's circular has had its say and there is no one left to read this but the man who writes it and the form that will outlive him:

I can release the engineer's statement now. To the District Seat, with the summary leaf, into the archive. It would not save her — she is gone, the verdict has no force, there is no proceeding left to reopen and no addressee left to acquit. But it would put the truth on the record. It would make the file say, after the fact, in cold ink, that the plant was the slow poisoner and the teacher was at most the panicked second hand, and that the State tried the gettable woman and never crossed the road to the gettable-but-better-documented man. It would clear her name in the only court left, which is the archive, where the dead and the gone are tried again by whoever opens the drawer in fifty years. It is the honest thing. It is, I have understood since the card came back, also the cheap thing — the courage that costs nothing, found the morning after it could have mattered, the confession a man makes once the confessing is safe. I held it when it would have helped her. To release it now, into an empty room, to a town that has stopped reading, would be to buy myself the feeling of an honest man at the one price I can finally afford: nothing.

Or I can hold it still — and a thing held one cycle, then another, then through a spring and a flood and a building going into a river, is not held. It is kept. It is consigned. It is in the Drawer whether I stamp it or not, and a man should name what he has done. So I have stamped it. Undeliverable. Not to clear her, because clearing her now is a performance for an empty house. And not to doom her, because there is no dooming left to do; she has unmade her own verdict by leaving, folded the blanket against it, walked the ice ahead of the State's slow hand. I consign it because I have, at last, understood the one thing the inspector understood about me from a cold memo and a warm rack: that I can no longer read my own measurement. I do not know whether releasing it would be justice or vanity. I do not know whether holding it is restraint or appetite. I have proven, twice on the record, in Cycle 9 and Cycle 21, that I can make her guilty or innocent at will by the order I deal the same true cards — and a man who has proven that has proven he is not fit to deal them, and the only honest move left to a dealer who cannot trust his own hand is to put the deck down. I am putting the deck down. I am taking my hand off the scale by refusing the last weight, and I know — I want it recorded that I know, so that no one mistakes this for innocence — that refusing the last weight is itself the heaviest thing I have done all winter, that non-delivery is a delivery decision, that I am not stepping out of the order. I am making the last arrangement and calling it the end of arranging. That is the curdle. I have read it on my own face in the dark glass of the terminal that never connects. There is no clean way down from a scaffold a man built himself.

Beside the statement I have put the envelope. 0431. It was never on the proceeding; it could not be undeliverable; I have made it undeliverable by hand, out of order, because I wanted them in the same drawer, the lever and the letter, the truth I would not release and the love I could not send, filed together at last where they have in fact always belonged, since the first were always the same thing: a paper kept warm by the stove because letting it go was the one thing this office made impossible for the man who runs it. She wrote that she did not need to know whether her reader was real. I needed to know whether she would stay if I delivered the truth, and the terrible answer the card gave me is that I will never find out, and that not-finding-out is what I have chosen, because as long as the lever is in the Drawer and not in the world, the file is not finished, the door is not shut, there remains one undelivered thing of hers on my rack — and I have spent my whole life learning that the way I keep what I love is by not sending it. I did it to Ana. I am doing it to the teacher I never met. The Drawer is where my loves go to stay mine, and I have just put the best of them in, and stamped it, and the stamp says undeliverable, and the stamp is the truest word in the file.

I wrote once — Cycle 1, on the very first slip, when this was a clever man's clever boast — *I have decided I am the order.* I have read that sentence the way I read hers, too many times, and I retract it. Let the record carry the retraction in the same violet as the boast. I have decided to stop being the order, because I no longer trust the man who is. Let it not arrive. Let her stay undecided, and gone, and free, and unread by the State that wanted to weigh her — and mine, in the only way I was ever able to keep anything, which is by not sending it. The post is the last thing in the Republic that still works. This morning I have made it stop working, once, on purpose, perfectly, with no forgery and no missing letter and no figure out of place, by doing the one thing a perfect post office is built to make unthinkable, which is to keep a true letter from arriving. The chain of custody is unbroken. Nothing is lost. Everything is exactly where I put it. And a woman will go unjudged to the end of the world, and a town will never be told the plant poisoned its water, and the only man who could have said so has filed the saying in a drawer and stamped it shut, and the record is clean, and the record is a lie the size of two lives, and both are true, and that is the order, and I am no longer it.

The Drawer is shut. The key is where it has been four years. There is nothing held against this proceeding. There is nothing to release. The stove is low and I am not going to feed it, the building being cold soon for good and the river patient and the clock long stopped at the minute the roof went.

Filed in good order. — G.E.


[Margin, G.E., in violet, at the foot of the closing slip — the last thing written into the file of The State v. Domnica Albu:]

The Drawer's inventory, set down for whoever opens it, the form requiring a manifest of the dead-letter and no one but the dead reading manifests: one engineer's statement, the truth, undelivered. One letter, D. Albu, Envelope 0431, undelivered. One anniversary letter, undelivered, four years, dated the 9th of February, which is tomorrow, which I did not plan and notice only as I write it and will not change, the river having taught me what to do with the things I cannot send. One summons, addressee deceased. One seed catalogue, no such address. The grief filed between a dead man and a garden, and now between the two of them, the wife I did not send and the woman I did not send, a teacher and a teacher's silence, and the seeds, which someone ordered, once, planning a spring, and never came to collect.

I am keeping all of it. It is the only correspondence of my life, and not one letter of it was ever posted, and it is, every undelivered page, in good order, which I used to think was the funniest sentence in the language and now know to be the cruelest, the two having turned out, like guilt and rescue, like mercy and cowardice, like the order received and the order true, to be one sentence read twice.

[STAMP: DEAD-LETTER DRAWER — CLOSED — CENTRAL SORTING, VÂLCOV]
[no SEEN stamp; the violet remains on ration; the State has not seen, and will not, this quarter or any, the thing this office decided in the dark]


[END OF THE CASE FILE]
